# Standard Unicode Emoji 17.0

- Source basis: Unicode Emoji 17.0 / CLDR order via Emojibase data 17.0.0
- Count: 3953 emoji entries - exclude some broken emoji
- Excluded: Private Use Area characters and standalone regional-indicator components
- Format: emoji  code  name
- Note: code values omit emoji variation selector U+FE0F to match common Unicode code notation, but the displayed emoji may include it for rendering.
